407
408
409inline cFontPtr NEW_CFONT_CALIBRI_24()
410{
411 cImage *img = new chai3d::cImage();
412 cLoadPNG(img, CFONT_CALIBRI_24_BYTEARRAY, sizeof(CFONT_CALIBRI_24_BYTEARRAY));
413
414 cFontPtr font = cFont::create();
415 font->m_charset.m_base = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET_BASE;
416 font->m_charset.m_lineHeight = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET_LINEHEIGHT;
417 font->m_charset.m_width = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_WIDTH;
418 font->m_charset.m_height = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_HEIGHT;
419 font->m_charset.m_pages = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET_PAGES;
420 for (int i=0; i<256; i++)
421 {
422 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_x = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET[8*i ];
423 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_y = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET[8*i+1];
424 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_width = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET[8*i+2];
425 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_height = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET[8*i+3];
426 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xOffset = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET[8*i+4];
427 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_yOffset = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET[8*i+5];
428 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xAdvance = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET[8*i+6];
429 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_page = CFONT_CALIBRI_24_CHARSET[8*i+7];
430 }
431 font->m_charset.preProcess();
432
433 font->m_texture->setImage(std::shared_ptr<chai3d::cImage>(img));
434
435 return (font);
436}
